				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
									<p class="" data-start="141" data-end="431">At Denny’s, our Specialty Pancakes &amp; Breakfasts are the perfect choice for those mornings when you’re craving something extra sweet and full of flavor. Whether you&#8217;re looking to indulge in something rich or prefer a lighter option, we have just what you need to make your breakfast special.</p><p class="" data-start="433" data-end="893">Start your day off right with our Cinnamon Roll Pancake Slam®—a warm, indulgent treat that’s a perfect blend of cinnamon and sweetness. Or dive into the Choconana Pancake Slam®, packed with layers of chocolatey goodness and fresh bananas, making every bite a delight. For those who enjoy a touch of fruit, our fruity pancakes with fresh berries are a refreshing way to start your morning, while those who like a bit of crunch can savor our other tasty options.</p><p class="" data-start="895" data-end="1220">If you’re in the mood for something a little lighter but still satisfying, our Hearty 9-Grain Pancake Slam® and the Berry Vanilla Crepe Breakfast are great choices. Each of these dishes comes with your favorite sides, like fluffy eggs, crispy bacon, or savory sausage, making them the perfect balance of flavor and nutrition.</p><p class="" data-start="1222" data-end="1567">Looking to share something fun with family or friends? Try our Maple Stuffed Donut Holes—a playful and delicious treat that’s perfect for passing around the table. No matter what you choose, Denny’s Specialty Pancakes &amp; Breakfasts are the perfect way to kick off your day with a meal that will leave you feeling satisfied and ready for anything.</p>								</div>

									<p class="" data-start="125" data-end="415">Denny’s Signature Breakfasts are designed to deliver bold flavors and comforting dishes in every bite. Whether you&#8217;re in the mood for a hearty Country Fried Steak &amp; Eggs, a flavorful T-Bone Steak &amp; Eggs, or the rich, slow-roasted Braised Beef Skillet, you’ll find a dish that hits the spot.</p><p class="" data-start="417" data-end="843">For something with a bit more zest, try the Cali Taco Skillet, packed with fresh veggies, eggs, and salsa verde, or the spicy Santa Fe Skillet featuring chorizo and seasoned potatoes. If you’re craving a satisfying sandwich, our Grand Slamwich® and Moons Over My Hammy® are fan favorites. These tasty creations offer a hearty combination of eggs, meat, and cheese on toasted artisan bread, served alongside crispy hash browns.</p><p class="" data-start="845" data-end="1136">If omelettes are what you’re after, we’ve got you covered with a variety of options. From the Ultimate Omelette® to the Philly Cheesesteak Omelette, or even the chance to Build Your Own Omelette, each one is loaded with fresh ingredients and served with hash browns and your choice of bread.</p>								</div>

				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
									<p class="" data-start="56" data-end="414">Denny’s breakfast sides are the perfect complement to any meal, offering a variety of delicious sweet and savory options to enhance your experience. If you&#8217;re in the mood for something indulgent, try our Berry Waffles drizzled with caramel sauce or the Berry Stuffed French Toast®, filled with creamy cream cheese—both guaranteed to satisfy your sweet tooth.</p><p class="" data-start="416" data-end="751">If you prefer something simpler but still satisfying, you can enjoy a classic Waffle, French Toast, or Strawberry Vanilla Crepes, each topped with seasonal berries and a generous helping of sweet sauce. For a heartier side, consider adding crispy Hash Browns, smoky Bacon, savory Sausage, or a perfectly grilled Ham Slice to your meal.</p><p class="" data-start="753" data-end="1094">For those looking for lighter options, we offer Fresh Seasonal Fruit and Eggs cooked just the way you like, along with classic sides like Biscuits and Gravy or Seasoned Red-Skinned Potatoes. Whether you&#8217;re craving something sweet, savory, or a combination of both, Denny’s breakfast sides are sure to satisfy whatever you&#8217;re in the mood for.</p>								</div>

				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
									<p class="" data-start="89" data-end="426">Start your meal with Denny’s tasty starters, perfect for sharing or enjoying all on your own. If you&#8217;re craving something savory, our Boneless Chicken Wings are a great choice, available in BBQ, Buffalo, or Nashville Hot sauce to suit your taste. Or, enjoy our golden, crispy Mozzarella Cheese Sticks, a fan favorite that’s always a hit.</p><p class="" data-start="428" data-end="769">If you’re looking for variety, our Classic Sampler has it all—crispy onion rings, mozzarella sticks, and wavy-cut fries, all served with your choice of dipping sauces to make every bite even better. For something tender and juicy, try our Premium Chicken Tenders, perfectly fried and paired with your favorite dipping sauce for extra flavor.</p><p class="" data-start="771" data-end="1074">For those in the mood for something bold, our Zesty Nachos are packed with seasoned ground beef, Pepper Jack queso, melted cheddar cheese, fresh pico de gallo, and a dollop of sour cream. Each starter is crafted with quality ingredients to satisfy your hunger and get your meal off to a delicious start.</p>								</div>

									<p class="" data-start="68" data-end="299">The <strong>$2/$4/$6/$8</strong> Value Menu offers a wide range of tasty and satisfying meals at prices that can’t be beat. Looking to start your day right? The Loaded Breakfast Sandwich and Super Slam™ have everything you need to kick off your morning.</p><p class="" data-start="590" data-end="768">For a timeless choice, the Classic Burger with Fries is always a winner. If you’re after something lighter, the Grilled Cheese with Soup or Side Salad is the perfect cozy option.</p><p class="" data-start="770" data-end="981">Want to make your meal even more satisfying? Add extra pancakes, French toast, or even cheesecake to your order. Affordable, delicious, and available all day—our Value Menu truly has something for every craving.</p>								</div>

        <div class="scrollbox">
            <h2>Introduction</h2>
            <p>Denny’s is one of the most recognized diner-style restaurants in the United States. Known for its all-day breakfast, family-friendly atmosphere, and comfort food, Denny’s has become a staple in many communities. Whether you’re craving pancakes at midnight or a hearty burger for lunch, Denny’s offers a wide variety of options that cater to different tastes.</p>
            
            <h2>History of Denny’s</h2>
            <p>Denny’s was founded in 1953 in Lakewood, California, as "Danny’s Donuts." The restaurant quickly expanded its offerings beyond donuts, rebranding as Denny’s in 1959. Over the decades, Denny’s has grown into a nationwide chain with over 1,600 locations, offering classic American diner food to customers across the country.</p>
            
            <h2>Finding a Denny’s Near You</h2>
            <p>When looking for a Denny’s nearby, you have multiple ways to find the closest location:</p>
            <ul>
                <li><strong>Denny’s Website</strong> – The official website (www.dennys.com) has a store locator feature where you can enter your zip code or city to find the nearest restaurant.</li>
                <li><strong>Google Maps</strong> – Simply type "Denny’s near me" in Google search or maps, and it will display nearby locations.</li>
                <li><strong>Denny’s Mobile App</strong> – Download the Denny’s app to locate restaurants, view menus, and place orders online.</li>
                <li><strong>Third-Party Apps</strong> – Apps like Yelp and TripAdvisor provide reviews and directions to nearby Denny’s locations.</li>
            </ul>
            
            <h2>Menu Highlights</h2>
            <p>Denny’s menu is diverse, catering to breakfast lovers, burger enthusiasts, and those looking for a quick bite. Some of the top menu items include:</p>
            <ul>
                <li><strong>Grand Slam Breakfast</strong> – A customizable meal featuring pancakes, eggs, bacon, and sausage.</li>
                <li><strong>Moons Over My Hammy</strong> – A famous ham and scrambled egg sandwich with Swiss and American cheese on grilled sourdough.</li>
                <li><strong>Double Cheeseburger</strong> – A juicy, classic burger served with fries.</li>
                <li><strong>Lumberjack Slam</strong> – A hearty breakfast with eggs, ham, bacon, sausage, pancakes, and toast.</li>
                <li><strong>Omelettes and Skillets</strong> – Various options featuring fresh vegetables, meats, and cheeses.</li>
            </ul>
            
            <h2>Denny’s Specials and Deals</h2>
            <p>Denny’s frequently offers promotions and discounts, including:</p>
            <ul>
                <li><strong>Value Menu</strong> – Affordable meal options for breakfast, lunch, and dinner.</li>
                <li><strong>Senior and Kids Discounts</strong> – Special pricing for seniors and kids.</li>
                <li><strong>Free Birthday Meal</strong> – Customers can enjoy a free meal on their birthday by signing up for Denny’s Rewards.</li>
                <li><strong>Late-Night Deals</strong> – Discounts on select menu items during late-night hours.</li>
            </ul>
            
            <h2>Denny’s 24/7 Service</h2>
            <p>One of the reasons Denny’s stands out from other restaurants is its 24/7 operation. Many Denny’s locations are open around the clock, making them a popular choice for late-night diners, truck drivers, and those looking for comfort food at any hour.</p>
            
            <h2>Denny’s Locations</h2>
            <p>Denny’s has locations in nearly every state in the U.S. and in several other countries. Some of the busiest locations include:</p>
            <ul>
                <li><strong>Las Vegas, Nevada</strong> – A popular spot for tourists and locals alike.</li>
                <li><strong>Orlando, Florida</strong> – Close to major attractions like Disney World and Universal Studios.</li>
                <li><strong>Los Angeles, California</strong> – One of the original Denny’s markets with several locations.</li>
                <li><strong>New York City, New York</strong> – Conveniently located in busy metropolitan areas.</li>
            </ul>

            <p>If you’re looking for a "Denny’s near me," you have plenty of options to find one quickly. With its extensive menu, 24/7 service, and affordable prices, Denny’s remains a go-to destination for breakfast, lunch, and dinner.</p>
